# Authored Function Reconstruction Priority List

Input: `text.hlil(19).txt`

## Method

- Parsed every HLIL function boundary by address/header.
- Excluded functions marked or inferred as non-authored/runtime support: MFC/import thunks, MSVC EH funclets, compiler-generated scalar-deleting destructors, decorated import symbols, ordinal thunks, and `sub_`/`__ehhandler_` support routines.
- Counted direct textual callees in HLIL and separated callees that resolve to other authored functions in this same file.
- Detected unresolved indirect member calls conservatively when visible as `->Function(...)`; these are not resolved to authored callee names.
- Sorted by dependency burden: direct leafs first, then functions with no authored callees, then functions with authored callees ordered by authored-callee count, total call-like count, HLIL size, and address.

## Summary

| Metric | Count |
|---|---:|
| Functions parsed | 4951 |
| Excluded non-authored/support functions | 1549 |
| Authored reconstruction candidates | 3402 |
| P0 leaf: no direct or detected indirect callees | 660 |
| P1 no authored callees: external/import/indirect only | 571 |
| P2+ has authored callees | 2171 |

## Priority buckets

- **P0**: first-pass reconstruction targets. No direct named callees and no detected `->Function(...)` indirect calls in HLIL.
- **P1**: next best targets. No direct authored callees, but calls imports, CRT/library functions, or unresolved indirect targets.
- **P2+**: has direct authored callees. These should generally wait until their listed authored callees are reconstructed.
